### [116] [CodeGraphVLP: Code-as-Planner Meets Semantic-Graph State for Non-Markovian Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22238)
*Khoa Vo,Sieu Tran,Taisei Hanyu,Yuki Ikebe,Duy Nguyen,Bui Duy Quoc Nghi,Minh Vu,Anthony Gunderman,Chase Rainwater,Anh Nguyen,Ngan Le*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的视觉-语言-动作(VLA)模型框架“CodeGraphVLP”，主要解决机器人在复杂长期任务下的信息缺失和混乱问题，使其能更可靠、高效地完成操作任务。该方法通过引入语义图持久存储任务关键信息，并结合代码式规划器与视觉-语言提示，有效提升了任务完成率并减少了规划延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLA模型往往被当作短时决策器，仅依赖最新观测作出行为决策，无法处理长期任务中的信息遮挡、回溯需求及视觉漂移等现实挑战。尤其在非马尔可夫（long-horizon, non-Markovian）情景下，如有用线索只在早期出现或当前被遮挡，传统方法难以完成任务。作者为提升真实环境下的机器人泛化与鲁棒性，提出了新的方法。

Method: 方法采用层次化结构，核心为语义图（semantic-graph），持续维护任务相关实体与关系（即便部分无法观测）。基于此，利用可执行的代码规划器进行高效任务进度检查，规划子任务及相关目标对象，通过聚焦关键证据抑制杂乱（clutter-suppressed observations），引导VLA执行器专注于关键信息。此外，结合进度指导的视觉-语言提示提升提示质量。

Conclusion: CodeGraphVLP为长期、多步骤机器人操作提供了更鲁棒、高效的方案，不仅在性能上超越现有强基线，还保证了规划效率。层次化语义状态和代码式规划的引入，为未来复杂机器人任务的泛化与可靠执行提供了新思路。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models promise generalist robot manipulation, but are typically trained and deployed as short-horizon policies that assume the latest observation is sufficient for action reasoning. This assumption breaks in non-Markovian long-horizon tasks, where task-relevant evidence can be occluded or appear only earlier in the trajectory, and where clutter and distractors make fine-grained visual grounding brittle. We present CodeGraphVLP, a hierarchical framework that enables reliable long-horizon manipulation by combining a persistent semantic-graph state with an executable code-based planner and progress-guided visual-language prompting. The semantic-graph maintains task-relevant entities and relations under partial observability. The synthesized planner executes over this semantic-graph to perform efficient progress checks and outputs a subtask instruction together with subtask-relevant objects. We use these outputs to construct clutter-suppressed observations that focus the VLA executor on critical evidence. On real-world non-Markovian tasks, CodeGraphVLP improves task completion over strong VLA baselines and history-enabled variants while substantially lowering planning latency compared to VLM-in-the-loop planning. We also conduct extensive ablation studies to confirm the contributions of each component.

</details>


### [117] [Learning Control Policies to Provably Satisfy Hard Affine Constraints for Black-Box Hybrid Dynamical Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22244)
*Aayushi Shrivastava,Kartik Nagpal,Sairam Jinkala,Jean-Baptiste Bouvier,Negar Mehr*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种能够在闭环系统中严格满足状态约束的强化学习方法，适用于只知道仿射重置映射、动力学为黑盒的混合动力系统。该方法通过设计仿射且具拒斥作用的策略，确保系统轨迹不会违反安全约束，并在状态跳变前后均进行了考虑。实验结果优于当前主流方法，并始终保证了安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 混合动力系统常存在非线性和未知动力学，且伴随瞬时状态跃迁。传统依赖动力学信息的安全约束方法如CBF和可达性分析难以适用。强化学习方法要么需动力学已知，要么仅靠奖励惩罚，对真正实现严格安全受限能力有限。需要一种对黑盒系统也能严格满意安全约束的RL方法。

Method: 提出将RL策略限定为仿射（线性）形式，且在接近约束边界时具备“拒斥”特性，使系统状态轨迹远离风险区域；针对混合系统中的重置映射/跳变，额外引入一层仿射拒斥区域，防止跳变后越界。推导满足安全约束的充分条件；在混合环境如摆系统与抛球系统中对比了现有强化学习、奖励塑形和CBF方法。

Result: 实验证明，在摆系统和抛球系统等典型混合动力环境中，该方法能学习到质量更高的RL策略，且始终严格满足安全约束，优于奖励塑形和CBF学习的方法。

Conclusion: 提出的方法在无需显式已知动力学的混合黑盒系统中，能保证强化学习策略始终严格符合状态约束；相较于现有方法，具有更强的安全性和策略质量，因此在实际具安全需求的自动控制领域应用潜力较大。

Abstract: Ensuring safety for black-box hybrid dynamical systems presents significant challenges due to their instantaneous state jumps and unknown explicit nonlinear dynamics. Existing solutions for strict safety constraint satisfaction, like control barrier functions (CBFs) and reachability analysis, rely on direct knowledge of the dynamics. Similarly, safe reinforcement learning (RL) approaches often rely on known system dynamics or merely discourage safety violations through reward shaping. In this work, we want to learn RL policies which provably satisfy affine state constraints in closed loop for black-box hybrid dynamical systems with affine reset maps. Our key insight is forcing the RL policy to be affine and repulsive near the constraint boundaries for the unknown nonlinear dynamics of the system, providing guarantees that the trajectories will not violate the constraint. We further account for constraint violation due to instantaneous state jumps that occur due to impacts or reset maps in the hybrid system by introducing a second repulsive affine region before the reset that prevents post-reset states from violating the constraint. We derive sufficient conditions under which these policies satisfy safety constraints in closed loop. We also compare our approach with state-of-the-art reward shaping and learned-CBF methods on hybrid dynamical systems like the constrained pendulum and paddle juggler environments. In both scenarios, we show that our methodology learns higher quality policies while always satisfying the safety constraints.

### [118] [False Feasibility in Variable Impedance MPC for Legged Locomotion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22251)
*Vishal Ramesh*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文分析了当前可变阻抗模型预测控制模型（MPC）在处理关节刚度时与实际物理可行性之间的偏差，提出了其理论基础并给出修正方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的MPC方法将关节刚度作为即时决策变量，但在实际一阶执行器动态下可实现的刚度范围比被建模的参数空间要小，存在实际不可实现的控制指令。迫切需要明确模型与现实之间的可行域区别，解决方案影响控制器性能和鲁棒性。

Method: 本文区分了参数域可行集（Fparam）与物理可实现集（Freal），提出并分析了两者的不匹配度量alpha（执行器带宽与任务时间尺度的无量纲参数）。针对1D跳跃单足机器人，通过理论推导和数值仿真验证，得到了关键阈值alpha_crit，指出当alpha低于门槛时，所有刚度指令都无法实现参数基预测，并进一步验证在平面弹簧载体倒立摆系统中的作用。

Result: 得出关键无量纲参数alpha_crit，低于该阈值时全部控制指令无法实现。数值仿真结果表明在十组参数下模型预测和实际可控性偏差呈单调增大，与理论预测高度一致（log-log R2=0.99）。还提出了更低的极限阈值alpha_infeas，证明即便收紧刚度上下限也无法补救。

Conclusion: 通过在状态预测中引入刚度状态，实现了可行性与预测的一致性。对MPC设计有指导意义，有助于解决结构调参保守性问题，并为机器人实施中的参数选型提供理论基础。

Abstract: Variable impedance model predictive control (MPC) formulations that treat joint stiffness as an instantaneous decision variable operate on a feasible set strictly larger than the physically realizable set under first-order actuator dynamics. We identify this as a formulation error rather than a modeling approximation, formalize the distinction between the parameter-based feasible set Fparam and the realizable set Freal, and characterize the regime of mismatch via the dimensionless parameter alpha = omega_sT (actuator bandwidth times task timescale). For the 1D hopping monoped, we prove that below an analytical threshold alpha_crit derived in closed form from task physics, no admissible stiffness command realizes the parameter-based prediction. Numerical validation in 1D shows monotonic deviation growth as alpha decreases, with the predicted scaling holding across ten parameter combinations (log-log R2 = 0.99). Mechanism transfer to planar spring-loaded inverted pendulum dynamics confirms center-of-mass and stance-timing deviation as the primary consequence, with regime-dependent friction effects as a tertiary observable. A second threshold alpha_infeas < alpha_crit establishes a floor below which restricting the admissible stiffness range cannot repair realizability, closing the conservative-tuning objection on structural grounds. Augmenting the prediction state with stiffness closes the mismatch by construction.

*HyoJae Kang,Yeong Jae Park,Hyunmok Jung,Joonho Lee,Dong Il Park*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机械手多关注手指自由度，忽略了手掌的运动对对掌能力的贡献。本研究旨在定量分析手掌自由度对提升拇指与其余手指出掌能力的影响，推动更优仿生机械手设计。

Method: 建立具有不同自由度分布的五指机器人手模型，通过在相邻手指间引入手掌运动，提出基于体素化指尖可达区域的重叠工作空间体积指标，分析了总自由度增加及重分配下共七种情况对对掌性能的影响。

Result: 实验表明，增加手掌自由度能显著提高无名指和小指与拇指的对掌能力，主要通过底座位置的变化实现。当总自由度受限时，自由度的重分配在扩大工作空间和运动学冗余性之间存在权衡。

Abstract: This study investigates the kinematic role of palm degrees of freedom (DoF) in enhancing thumb opposability in a five-finger robotic hand. A hand model consisting of a five DoF thumb and four fingers with three to four DoF is analyzed, where palm motion is introduced between adjacent fingers. To quantitatively evaluate thumb-finger interaction, the overlap workspace volume is defined based on voxelized fingertip reachable regions. Seven cases are considered, including configurations with increased total DoF and configurations in which the total DoF is maintained by redistributing DoF from the fingers to the palm. The results show that palm DoF significantly improves opposability, particularly for the ring and little fingers, by repositioning their base locations rather than simply extending their reachable range. However, when the total DoF is constrained, redistributing DoF to the palm leads to trade-offs between overlap workspace expansion and kinematic redundancy. These findings indicate that palm DoF and finger DoF play distinct roles in hand kinematics and should be considered jointly in design. This study provides a quantitative framework for evaluating palm-induced opposability without relying on object or contact models and offers practical design guidelines for incorporating palm motion in robotic hands.

### [122] [Information-Theoretic Geometry Optimization and Physics-Aware Learning for Calibration-Free Magnetic Localization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22526)
*Wenxuan Xie,Yuelin Zhang,Qingpeng Ding,Jianghua Chen,Jiewen Tan,Jiwei Shan,Shing Shin Cheng*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法包括两部分：1）用FIM评估体系优化并提出“错层分割阵列”传感器几何，实现对永磁体的高可观测性无障碍外部部署；2）以此优化的传感配置，提出了Phy-GAANet网络，采用物理感知特征（PIF）和几何感知注意力（GAA），基于硬件感知的合成数据端到端训练，无需校准，显著提升了仿真到真实的泛化能力。

Abstract: Wireless localization of permanent magnets enables occlusion-free guidance for medical interventions, yet its practical accuracy is fundamentally limited by two coupled challenges: the poor observability of conventional planar sensor arrays and the simulation-to-reality (Sim-to-Real) gap of learning-based estimators. To address these issues, this article presents a unified framework that combines information-theoretic sensor geometry optimization with physics-aware deep learning. First, a rigorous Fisher Information Matrix (FIM)-based evaluation framework is established to quantify geometry-induced observability limitations. The results show that a staggered split-array topology provides a substantially stronger observability foundation for localization while remaining compatible with practical external deployment. Second, building on this optimized sensing configuration, we propose Phy-GAANet, a calibration-free estimator trained entirely on hardware-aware synthetic data. By incorporating Physics-Informed Features (PIF) for saturation modeling and Geometry-Aware Attention (GAA) for preserving cross-layer vector structure, the network effectively bridges the Sim-to-Real gap. Extensive real-world experiments demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, achieving a position error of 1.84 mm and an orientation error of 3.18 degrees at a refresh rate exceeding 270 Hz. The proposed method consistently outperforms classical Levenberg--Marquardt solvers and generic convolutional baselines, particularly in suppressing catastrophic outliers and maintaining robustness in challenging near-field boundary regions. Beyond the proposed network, the FIM-guided analysis also provides a framework for sensor geometry design in magnetic localization systems under practical deployment constraints.

### [124] [RedVLA: Physical Red Teaming for Vision-Language-Action Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22591)
*Yuhao Zhang,Borong Zhang,Jiaming Fan,Jiachen Shen,Yishuai Cai,Yaodong Yang,Jiaming Ji*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于检测视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型物理安全风险的red teaming框架RedVLA，可系统性发现模型在实际部署前的各类物理不安全行为，并通过实验验证了其有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型在现实物理环境中的应用受限于潜在不可控的物理安全风险，现有机制难以及时发现这些部署前的安全隐患，亟需主动检测手段。

Method: RedVLA采用两阶段流程：（1）风险场景合成，自动定位常规操作中的关键交互区，布置具风险性的因素以引发模型的不安全行为；（2）风险放大，通过无需梯度的优化方式强化风险因素，提高触发不安全行为的稳定性和通用性。

Result: RedVLA在六种主流VLA模型上的实验显示能发现多样的不安全行为，且经过不超过10次优化迭代即可使攻击成功率（ASR）最高达95.5%。此外，作者还提出了以RedVLA生成数据为基础的轻量级安全防护方案SimpleVLA-Guard。

Conclusion: RedVLA为VLA模型物理安全红队测试提供了系统化检测手段，显著提升了安全风险的发现效率，有望推动VLA模型在实际物理世界中的安全可控应用。

Abstract: The real-world deployment of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models remains limited by the risk of unpredictable and irreversible physical harm. However, we currently lack effective mechanisms to proactively detect these physical safety risks before deployment. To address this gap, we propose \textbf{RedVLA}, the first red teaming framework for physical safety in VLA models. We systematically uncover unsafe behaviors through a two-stage process: (I) \textbf{Risk Scenario Synthesis} constructs a valid and task-feasible initial risk scene. Specifically, it identifies critical interaction regions from benign trajectories and positions the risk factor within these regions, aiming to entangle it with the VLA's execution flow and elicit a target unsafe behavior. (II) \textbf{Risk Amplification} ensures stable elicitation across heterogeneous models. It iteratively refines the risk factor state through gradient-free optimization guided by trajectory features. Experiments on six representative VLA models show that RedVLA uncovers diverse unsafe behaviors and achieves the ASR up to 95.5\% within 10 optimization iterations. To mitigate these risks, we further propose SimpleVLA-Guard, a lightweight safety guard built from RedVLA-generated data. Our data, assets, and code are available \href{https://redvla.github.io}{here}.

</details>


### [125] [GazeVLA: Learning Human Intention for Robotic Manipulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22615)
*Chengyang Li,Kaiyi Xiong,Yuan Xu,Lei Qian,Yizhou Wang,Wentao Zhu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了通过建模与迁移人类意图（基于视线信息）来提升机器人操作能力的方法，该模型在多个基准上实现了比现有方法更好的泛化性和性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前具身基础模型在机器人操作任务有突破性进展，但仍高度依赖大量机器人示范。为降低对机器人大量示范的依赖，引入了利用人类数据的尝试，然而由于人机间的具身差异，如何高效迁移知识仍是挑战。作者认为人类行为背后的“意图”有望成为弥合人机差异的中介表征。

Method: 作者提出了一个新颖框架，通过显式地学习和迁移人类意图来促进机器人操作。具体做法是将人类“意图”通过视线数据进行建模，先在大规模以第一视角采集的人类数据集上预训练意图及其与动作的协同关系，然后在少量人类和机器人数据上微调。推理阶段，模型采用链式思维推理范式，先预测意图后再执行动作。

Result: 实验在仿真和真实环境下、多种长时序和细粒度任务、few-shot和鲁棒性等基准上，表明该方法较现有强基线有更好的表现与泛化能力，并达到SOTA水平。

Conclusion: 通过显式学习和迁移基于视线的人类意图，有效提升了机器人操作的泛化和性能，降低了对大规模机器人示范的依赖，为弥合人机间的具身差异提供了一种可行途径。

Abstract: Embodied foundation models have achieved significant breakthroughs in robotic manipulation, yet they still depend heavily on large-scale robot demonstrations. Although recent works have explored leveraging human data to alleviate this dependency, effectively extracting transferable knowledge remains a significant challenge due to the inherent embodiment gap between human and robot. We argue that the intention underlying human actions can serve as a powerful intermediate representation for bridging this gap. In this paper, we introduce a novel framework that explicitly learns and transfers human intention to facilitate robotic manipulation. Specifically, we model intention through gaze, as it naturally precedes physical actions and serves as an observable proxy for human intent. Our model is first pretrained on a large-scale egocentric human dataset to capture human intention and its synergy with action, followed by finetuning on a small set of robot and human data. During inference, the model adopts a Chain-of-Thought reasoning paradigm, sequentially predicting intention before executing the action. Extensive evaluations in simulation and real-world settings, across long-horizon and fine-grained tasks, and under few-shot and robustness benchmarks, show that our method consistently outperforms strong baselines, generalizes better, and achieves state-of-the-art performance.

</details>


### [126] [ATRS: Adaptive Trajectory Re-splitting via a Shared Neural Policy for Parallel Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22715)
*Jiajun Yu,Guodong Liu,Li Wang,Pengxiang Zhou,Wentao Liu,Yin He,Chao Xu,Fei Gao,Yanjun Cao*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种结合深度强化学习与并行ADMM的自适应轨迹优化框架ATRS，通过智能地在线分割问题子区段，有效加速了高约束环境下的运动规划收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有并行ADMM轨迹优化方法通常将问题基于固定结构分解成子问题，但这种刚性结构在高度约束场景下容易出现部分子问题收敛缓慢，从而拖慢整体收敛速度。如何在优化过程中自适应地对“滞后”区段进行再分割，并有效决策何时、何地及如何分割，是当前方法难以解决的难题。

Method: 作者提出ATRS框架，将一个共享的深度强化学习策略嵌入到并行ADMM迭代中，采用多智能体共享策略的MDP建模，使每个轨迹区段作为同质智能体共享同一个策略网络。在每一步中，通过Confidence-Based Election机制，只有收敛最慢的区段被选择进行再分割。此外，策略仅依赖数值求解器的内部状态，无需场景几何信息，从而具备环境泛化能力。

Result: 仿真实验显示，ATRS可使迭代次数降低最多26%，计算时间减少19.1%。实物实验也验证了方法在大规模离线规划和实时板载重规划中的有效性，每轮周期只需35ms且无虚实差异。

Conclusion: ATRS方法在轨迹优化场景下有效提升了优化效率和收敛速度，并具备良好的泛化能力和实际部署价值，适用于不同规模和不同环境的高效运动规划。

Abstract: Parallel trajectory optimization via the Alternating Direction Method of Multipliers (ADMM) has emerged as a scalable approach to long-horizon motion planning. However, existing frameworks typically decompose the problem into parallel subproblems based on a predefined fixed structure. Such structural rigidity often causes optimization stagnation in highly constrained regions, where a few lagging subproblems delay global convergence. A natural remedy is to adaptively re-split these stagnating segments online. Yet, deciding when, where, and how to split exceeds the capability of rule-based heuristics. To this end, we propose ATRS, a novel framework that embeds a shared Deep Reinforcement Learning policy into the parallel ADMM loop. We formulate this adaptive adjustment as a Multi-Agent Shared-Policy Markov Decision Process, where all trajectory segments act as homogeneous agents and share a unified neural policy network. This parameter-sharing architecture endows the system with size invariance, enabling it to handle dynamically changing segment counts during re-splitting and generalize to arbitrary trajectory lengths. Furthermore, our formulation inherently supports zero-shot generalization to unseen environments, as our network relies solely on the internal states of the numerical solver rather than on the geometric features of the environment. To ensure solver stability, a Confidence-Based Election mechanism selects only the most stagnating segment for re-splitting at each step. Extensive simulations demonstrate that ATRS accelerates convergence, reducing the number of iterations by up to 26.0% and the computation time by up to 19.1%. Real-world experiments further confirm its applicability to both large-scale offline global planning and real-time onboard replanning within 35 ms per cycle, with no sim-to-real degradation.

</details>


### [127] [GCImOpt: Learning efficient goal-conditioned policies by imitating optimal trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22724)
*Jon Goikoetxea,Jesús F. Palacián*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的高效目标条件强化学习方法GCImOpt，通过轨迹优化生成高质量示范数据，训练出高性能且高效率的控制策略，适用于多种控制任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模仿学习依赖于示范数据，而这些数据昂贵且往往不够优质。本文旨在解决示范数据难获取或质量不高的问题，提升目标条件控制策略的实用性和泛化能力。

Method: 提出一种基于轨迹优化的数据生成方法，可在普通计算机上高效生成成千上万条最优轨迹，用作目标条件策略的训练数据。同时，采用数据增强策略，将中间状态作为额外目标，显著扩增训练集。然后利用这些数据训练神经网络，实现任意目标的控制。

Result: 在多个任务（如倒立摆、二维与三维四旋翼、6自由度机械臂等）上，训练得到的神经网络政策具有高成功率，控制效果接近最优。且模型小巧（<8万参数）、推理速度极快（比传统轨迹优化快6000倍），适合资源受限平台部署。实验结果表明方法具备普适性和实用性。

Conclusion: GCImOpt能够高效、大规模生成高质量演示数据，并训练出高性能、可泛化且高效的目标条件政策，极大降低了控制任务中模仿学习的门槛，适合实际嵌入式应用，具有广泛的推广潜力。

Abstract: Imitation learning is a well-established approach for machine-learning-based control. However, its applicability depends on having access to demonstrations, which are often expensive to collect and/or suboptimal for solving the task. In this work, we present GCImOpt, an approach to learn efficient goal-conditioned policies by training on datasets generated by trajectory optimization. Our approach for dataset generation is computationally efficient, can generate thousands of optimal trajectories in minutes on a laptop computer, and produces high-quality demonstrations. Further, by means of a data augmentation scheme that treats intermediate states as goals, we are able to increase the training dataset size by an order of magnitude. Using our generated datasets, we train goal-conditioned neural network policies that can control the system towards arbitrary goals. To demonstrate the generality of our approach, we generate datasets and then train policies for various control tasks, namely cart-pole stabilization, planar and three-dimensional quadcopter stabilization, and point reaching using a 6-DoF robot arm. We show that our trained policies can achieve high success rates and near-optimal control profiles, all while being small (less than 80,000 neural network parameters) and fast enough (up to more than 6,000 times faster than a trajectory optimization solver) that they could be deployed onboard resource-constrained controllers. We provide videos, code, datasets and pre-trained policies under a free software license; see our project website https://jongoiko.github.io/gcimopt/.

</details>
